We want to formilise in HoTT the intuition behind a correspondance between the
concept of *PathOver* and its respective *total space*. The term PathOver was
briefly mentioned in {% cite hottbook %} and later defined in {% cite Licata2015
%}. It is extensivily used in {%cite hott-in:agda %}.

![](/assets/png-images/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers-7f9fb342.png)

Let's review first an equility type that is closely relted with these pathovers.
(See also {% cite Licata2015 %} for some extra comments).

{: .foldable}

## Homogeneous equality

> `Path {A} a₀ a₁` is sometimes called **homogeneous equality**, because it
> relates two elements a₀ and a₁ whose types are *definitionally/judgementally
> equal*.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1026" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="1032" class="Number">30</a> <a id="1035" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>

## Heterogeneous equality

> In {%cite McBride2004 %} the author introduced a *heterogeneous equality*, which is an equality type
> `a:A= b:B` that relates two elements `a:A` and `b:B` which may have two judgementally
> distinct types, though the reflexivity constructor applies only when both the
> two types and the two terms are judgementally equal.

> However, McBride’s heterogeneous equality is **logically equivalent** to a
> homogeneous equality type *satisfying uniqueness of identity proofs*, which
> is undesirable **in homotopy type theory, because not all types should be sets**.

> This heterogeneous equality relates two elements of two different types along a
> specific equality α between the types.

We will continue using `idp` for the reflexivity constructor, which it's going
to be convenient to switch between the definitions of the heterogeneous equality
and furtermore, between the definition of the homogeneous equality.

Coercion along a homogeneous equality

  <a id="9500" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="9507" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9507" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="9516" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9517" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9520" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9520" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9522" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9525" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9525" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9529" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="9536" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9538" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9539" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9543" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9525" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9545" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9547" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9552" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9520" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9554" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9556" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="9566" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
    <a id="9646" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
    <a id="hott.Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="9688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9688" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="9697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9700" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9700" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9702" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9702" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9704" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9706" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="9708" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9708" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9712" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9525" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9713" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9715" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9717" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9539" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9708" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9720" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9723" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9725" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9730" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9734" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9736" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9520" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9738" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="13266" class="Comment">-- Application of an homotopy</a>

    <a id="13369" class="Comment">-- The axiom of function extensionality postulates that the</a>
    <a id="13433" class="Comment">-- application of homotopies is an equivalence.</a>

  <a id="16176" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="16183" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16183" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="16196" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="16207" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
    <a id="16278" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
    <a id="hott.Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="16295" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16295" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="16302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16304" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="16306" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16306" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16307" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="16310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16311" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16313" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16306" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16321" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16323" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16306" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

    <a id="23538" class="Comment">-- Half-adjointness implies equivalence.</a>
    <a id="hott.Halfadjoints.ishae-≃"></a><a id="23583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23583" class="Function">ishae-≃</a> <a id="23591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23593" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23594" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20905" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23600" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20919" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23603" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23605" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20983" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="23613" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23594" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23615" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23617" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20905" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#12178" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="23621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#20919" class="Bound">B</a>

    <a id="26336" class="Comment">-- Quasiinverses create equivalences.</a>

       <a id="27966" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2836" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="27970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27562" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="27978" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27890" class="Bound">α</a><a id="27979" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3247" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="27983" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2836" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="27987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27890" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="27993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4010" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="27997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#13686" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="28004" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#12984" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="28021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27890" class="Bound">α</a><a id="28022" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4010" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

  <a id="28047" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28052" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#26758" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a> <a id="28075" class="Keyword">public</a>

Let be `α : A == B`, `a : A`, and `b : B` then the following types are equivalent
to `HEq`.

### Equivalences

  <a id="28734" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28734" class="Function">HEq₁-to-HEq₂</a> <a id="28747" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28750" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28750" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="28752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28754" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28700" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28756" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="28759" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28713" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28760" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="28762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28762" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="28764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28766" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28700" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28767" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="28769" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28769" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="28771" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28713" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28774" class="Symbol">}</a>

Finally, we complete the chain of equivalence with `HEq₄-≃-HEq₁`.

{: .foldable}

For the follwing discussion, we may use heterogeneous using the first definition.

## Path over a path

The PathOver is the depedent version of a *path*, what it exactly means is that
we have a path between two endpoints from maybe different types but with. Which
is exactly the same definition of the heterogeneous equality. The difference is
that PathOvers simplifies the `HEq` definition by factorizing the type family
that is involved in the paths.

We first define `PathOver₁` as the inductive family with only one constructor,
the reflexivity over the reflexivity on the base space `A`. To eliminate this
type, we can use path-over induction. In Agda, we just do pattern matching on
the path in the base `A`. We can also define this notion of PathOvers in at least
other four different ways. Let's such definitions all equivalent.

- <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="33046" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="PathOver₁"></a><a id="33051" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33051" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a> <a id="33061" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33062" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33062" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="33065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33065" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33067" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33069" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33070" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33070" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33072" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33074" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="33078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33062" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="33080" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33083" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="33085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33070" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33089" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33091" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="33096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33065" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33098" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33100" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33101" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33101" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="33104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33070" class="Bound">A</a><a id="33107" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33109" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="33117" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33118" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="33121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33123" - <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver₅"></a><a id="33921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="33931" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33933" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="33935" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33936" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33936" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="33939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33939" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33941" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33943" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33944" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33946" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33948" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="33953" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33936" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="33955" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="33957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33957" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="33959" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33961" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33944" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33963" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33965" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="33970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33939" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33974" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33975" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="33978" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33978" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="33981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33983" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33944" class="Bound">A</a><a id="33984" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="33996" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33998" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33999" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="34001" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34003" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33975" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="34006" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="34009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33978" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="34011" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34014" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34017" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34019" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33957" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33975" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="34023" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="34025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34025" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="34028" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34030" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33957" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34032" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33978" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="34034" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34036" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34043" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33939" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a>
<a id="34046" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="34056" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34057" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="34059" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34061" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34061" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34062" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34064" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34064" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34066" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="34070" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34070" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34073" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="34076" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34070" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="34084" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34073" class="Bound">c₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Above when we used `transport C α c₁`, we could also have used `coe (ap C α)`,
both functions are of type `C a₁ → C a₂`. The other case with `c₂` is similar.

### Equivalences

{: .foldable}

    <a id="39710" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="39722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39722" class="Function">PathOver₅~PathOver₁</a> <a id="39742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39744" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39745" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39745" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="39747" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33051" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a> <a id="39759" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#38973" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="39761" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="39765" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39573" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="39768" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39577" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="39770" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="39782" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39784" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#38998" class="Function">PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁</a> <a id="39807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39808" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39201" class="Function">PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅</a> <a id="39831" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39745" class="Bound">p</a><a id="39832" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39834" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="39837" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39745" class="Bound">p</a>
      <a id="39845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39722" class="Function">PathOver₅~PathOver₁</a> <a id="39865" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33187" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="39869" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39871" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

      <a id="39882" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39882" class="Function">PathOver₁~PathOver₅</a> <a id="39902" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39905" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39905" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="39907" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="39919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#38973" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="39921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="39925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39573" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="39928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39577" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="39930" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="39942" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39201" class="Function">PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅</a> <a id="39967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#38998" class="Function">PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁</a> <a id="39991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39905" class="Bound">p</a><a id="39992" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39994" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="39997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39905" class="Bound">p</a>
      <a id="40005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39882" class="Function">PathOver₁~PathOver₅</a> <a id="40025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="40029" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40031" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We are going to use the fifth definition for pathovers, the one which is
using an inductive family. Nevertheless, in the following, the reader can change
the subindex of the `PathOver` word to use any other definition.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="40280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="40289" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33921" class="Function">PathOver₅</a>

<a id="40302" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="40308" class="Number">30</a> <a id="40311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="40320" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="40327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="40344" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>


> While we have motivated PathOver as a factored heterogeneous equality, there
> is also a geometric intuition. **Dependent types correspond to fibrations**, so a
> type `C : A → Type` can be pictured as its total space `∑ a:A . C` a projecting
> down to `A` by first projection.

> A **path-over** `γ : PathOver C α c­₁ c₂` represents a path σ in `∑ a:A . C` a
> a between `(a₁, c₁)` and `(a₂,c₂)`, such that ap fst σ is exactly `α`. That
> is, it is a path in the total space that projects down to, or lies over, `α`
> (path pairing `pair= α γ` will be made precise below)


## Total spaces

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="40983" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="40990" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40990" class="Module">_</a> <a id="40992" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40993" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="40996" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40996" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="40998" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41000" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41000" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="41009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40993" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="41011" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41015" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41017" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41000" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#761" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="41026" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40996" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="41028" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41030" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="41036" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41000" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41039" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41041" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="41050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41050" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="41061" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41063" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41064" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41064" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41066" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41068" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41071" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41076" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41078" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41081" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="41087" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41089" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41089" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41098" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="41161" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41078" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41166" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">==</a> <a id="41169" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41089" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">[</a> <a id="41174" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">↓</a>  <a id="41179" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41064" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41181" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="41185" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41050" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="41196" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41197" class="Argument">c₁</a> <a id="41200" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41202" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41202" class="Bound">c₁</a><a id="41204" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41211" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2816" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41216" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41218" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41220" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

  <a id="41227" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41227" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="41238" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41240" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41241" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41241" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41243" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41248" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41253" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41255" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41258" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41260" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="41264" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41266" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41266" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41269" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41271" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41273" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41275" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41281" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41283" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41284" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41284" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="41286" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41288" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41255" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">==</a> <a id="41294" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41266" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">[</a> <a id="41299" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41013" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="41303" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41241" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41305" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40280" class="Function">]</a><a id="41306" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="41312" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2736" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="41316" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="41318" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41030" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2816" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41255" class="Bound">c₁</a><a id="41325" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41033" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="41334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2816" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41336" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41266" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="41338" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="41341" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="41344" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41344" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="41346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41348" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="41352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2836" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="41356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41344" class="Bound">q</a><a id="41357" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41359" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1045" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41241" class="Bound">α</a><a id="41363" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="41367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41227" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="41378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41382" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41388" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2816" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1099" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41400" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="41405" class="Comment">-- -- more explict:</a>
  <a id="41427" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {idp}{c₁}{c₂} idp = (idp {a = (a₁ , c₁)}, idp {a = idp {a = a₁}})</a>

  <a id="41510" class="Comment">-- -- Alternative (also type-checked):</a>
  <a id="41551" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {α = α} γ = (pair= α γ , ap-fst-pair= α γ)</a>
  <a id="41610" class="Comment">--   where</a>
  <a id="41623" class="Comment">--   pair= : ∀ {i j} {A : Type i} {C : A → Type j}</a>
  <a id="41676" class="Comment">--     {a₁ a₂ : A} {c₁ : C a₁} {c₂ : C a₂}</a>
  <a id="41721" class="Comment">--     → (α : a₁ == a₂)</a>
  <a id="41747" class="Comment">--     → (γ : c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ])</a>
  <a id="41783" class="Comment">--     ------</a>
  <a id="41799" class="Comment">--     → (a₁ , c₁) == (a₂ , c₂)</a>
  <a id="41833" class="Comment">--   pair= idp γ = ap (_ ,_) γ</a>
  <a id="41866" class="Comment">--</a>
  <a id="41871" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= : (α : a₁ == a₂)</a>
  <a id="41908" class="Comment">--       → {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂} (γ : c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ] )</a>
  <a id="41970" class="Comment">--       → ap fst (pair= α γ) == α</a>
  <a id="42007" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= idp idp = idp</a>

## Other facts

We can build a dependent path by applying a depedent function to a homogeneous path.
